title: Language reference

h2. Liquidsoap scripting language reference

h3. Categories

The **Source / ...** categories contain all functions that return sources.
The **Input** functions are those which build elementary sources
(playing files, synthesizing sound, etc.).
The **Output** functions are those which take a source and register it
for being streamed to the outside (file, soundcard, audio server, etc.).
The **Visualization** functions are experimental ones that let you 
visualize in real-time some aspects of the audio stream.
The **Sound Processing** functions are those which basically work on the source 
as a continuous audio stream. They would typically be mixers of streams,
audio effects or analysis.
Finally, **Track Processing** functions are basically all 
others, often having a behaviour that depends on or affects the extra 
information that liquidsoap puts in streams: track limits and metadata.

* "Source / Conversions":#Source___Conversions
* "Source / Input":#Source___Input
* "Source / Liquidsoap":#Source___Liquidsoap
* "Source / MIDI Processing":#Source___MIDI_Processing
* "Source / Output":#Source___Output
* "Source / Sound Processing":#Source___Sound_Processing
* "Source / Sound Synthesis":#Source___Sound_Synthesis
* "Source / Track Processing":#Source___Track_Processing
* "Source / Video Processing":#Source___Video_Processing
* "Source / Visualization":#Source___Visualization
* "Bool":#Bool
* "Control":#Control
* "Interaction":#Interaction
* "Liquidsoap":#Liquidsoap
* "List":#List
* "Math":#Math
* "Pair":#Pair
* "String":#String
* "System":#System


h3@Source___Conversions. Source / Conversions
h5@audio_to_stereo. audio_to_stereo
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio=*+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Convert any kind of audio source into a stereo source.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=*+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>)

h5@drop_audio. drop_audio
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio=0,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Drop all audio channels of a stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@drop_midi. drop_midi
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

Drop all midi channels of a stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@drop_video. drop_video
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video=0,midi='#c)</pre>

Drop all video channels of a stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@id. id
<pre>(?id:string,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Does not do anything, simply forwards its input stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@mean. mean
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio=1,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Produce mono audio by taking the mean of all audio channels.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@mux_audio. mux_audio
<pre>(?id:string,audio:source(audio='#a,video=0,midi=0),
 source(audio=0,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Mux an audio stream into an audio-free stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>audio</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video=0,midi=0)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=0,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@mux_mono. mux_mono
<pre>(?id:string,mono:source(audio=1,video=0,midi=0),
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Mux a mono audio stream into another stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>mono</code> (<code>source(audio=1,video=0,midi=0)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@mux_stereo. mux_stereo
<pre>(?id:string,stereo:source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0),
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a+2,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Mux a stereo audio stream into another stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>stereo</code> (<code>source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@mux_video. mux_video
<pre>(?id:string,video:source(audio=0,video='#a,midi=0),
 source(audio='#b,video=0,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#b,video='#a,midi='#c)</pre>

Add video channnels to a stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>video</code> (<code>source(audio=0,video='#a,midi=0)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#b,video=0,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@stereo_left. stereo.left
<pre>(source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio=1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Extract the left channel of a stereo source

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</code>): Source to extract from

h5@stereo_right. stereo.right
<pre>(source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio=1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Extract the right channel of a stereo source

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</code>): Source to extract from

h5@swap. swap
<pre>(?id:string,source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Swap two channels of a stereo source.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</code>)



h3@Source___Input. Source / Input
h5@blank. blank
<pre>(?id:string,?duration:float)->source('a)</pre>

Produce silence and blank images.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>duration</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Duration of blank tracks in seconds, default means forever.

h5@empty. empty
<pre>(?id:string)->source(audio='a,video='b,midi='c)</pre>

A source that does not produce anything. No silence, no track at all.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.

h5@fail. fail
<pre>(?id:string)->source('b)</pre>

Creates a source that fails to produce anything.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)

h5@gstreamer_hls. gstreamer.hls
<pre>(?id:string,'a)->source(audio=2,video=1,midi=0)</pre>

Play an http live stream.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>'a</code>): URI of the HLS stream index.

h5@in. in
<pre>(?id:string,?start:bool,?on_start:(()->unit),
 ?on_stop:(()->unit),?fallible:bool)->
source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Create a source from the first available input driver in pulseaudio, portaudio, oss, alsa, blank.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>)
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>)
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>)

h5@input_external. input.external
<pre>(?id:string,?buffer:float,?channels:int,?max:float,
 ?restart:bool,?restart_on_error:bool,?samplerate:int,
 string)->source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Stream data from an external application.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>channels</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>2</code>): Number of channels.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>restart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Restart process when exited.
* <code>restart_on_error</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Restart process when exited with error.
* <code>samplerate</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>44100</code>): Samplerate.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Command to execute.

h5@input_external_avi. input.external.avi
<pre>(?id:string,?buffer:float,?max:float,?restart:bool,
 ?restart_on_error:bool,string)->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>
WARNING: This is only EXPERIMENTAL!

Stream data from an external application.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>restart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Restart process when exited.
* <code>restart_on_error</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Restart process when exited with error.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Command to execute.

h5@input_external_rawvideo. input.external.rawvideo
<pre>(?id:string,?buffer:float,?max:float,?restart:bool,
 ?restart_on_error:bool,string)->
source(audio=0,video=1,midi=0)</pre>
WARNING: This is only EXPERIMENTAL!

Stream data from an external application.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>restart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Restart process when exited.
* <code>restart_on_error</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Restart process when exited with error.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Command to execute.

h5@input_ffmpeg_video. input.ffmpeg.video
<pre>(?id:string,?restart:bool,?restart_on_error:bool,
 ?buffer:float,?max:float,?format:string,string)->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

No documentation available.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"input.ffmpeg.video"</code>)
* <code>restart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>restart_on_error</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>)
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.2</code>)
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>)
* <code>format</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>)

h5@input_gstreamer_audio. input.gstreamer.audio
<pre>(?id:string,?max:float,?pipeline:string)->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Stream audio from a GStreamer pipeline.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>pipeline</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"audiotestsrc"</code>): GStreamer pipeline to input from.

h5@input_gstreamer_audio_video. input.gstreamer.audio_video
<pre>(?id:string,?audio_pipeline:string,?max:float,
 ?pipeline:string,?video_pipeline:string)->
source(audio=2,video=1,midi=0)</pre>

Stream audio+video from a GStreamer pipeline.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>audio_pipeline</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"audiotestsrc"</code>): Audio pipeline to input from.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>pipeline</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Main GStreamer pipeline.
* <code>video_pipeline</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"videotestsrc"</code>): Video pipeline to input from.

h5@input_gstreamer_video. input.gstreamer.video
<pre>(?id:string,?max:float,?pipeline:string)->
source(audio=0,video=1,midi=0)</pre>

Stream video from a GStreamer pipeline.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>pipeline</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"videotestsrc"</code>): GStreamer pipeline to input from.

h5@input_harbor. input.harbor
<pre>(?id:string,?auth:((string,string)->bool),?buffer:float,
 ?debug:bool,?dumpfile:string,?icy:bool,
 ?icy_metadata_charset:string,?logfile:string,?max:float,
 ?metadata_charset:string,
 ?on_connect:(([(string*string)])->unit),
 ?on_disconnect:(()->unit),?password:string,?port:int,
 ?replay_metadata:bool,?timeout:float,?user:string,
 string)->source('a)</pre>

Retrieves the given http stream from the harbor.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>auth</code> (<code>(string,string)->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_,_) -> false</code>): Authentication function. <code>f(login,password)</code> returns <code>true</code> if the user should be granted access for this login. Override any other method if used.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>debug</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Run in debugging mode by not catching some exceptions.
* <code>dumpfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Dump stream to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>icy</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Enable ICY (shoutcast) protocol.
* <code>icy_metadata_charset</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): ICY (shoutcast) metadata charset. Guessed if empty. Default for shoutcast is ISO-8859-1. Set to that value if all your clients send metadata using this charset and automatic detection is not working for you.
* <code>logfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Log buffer status to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>metadata_charset</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Metadata charset for non-ICY (shoutcast) source protocols. Guessed if empty.
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): Function to execute when a source is connected. Its receives the list of headers, of the form: (<label>,<value>). All labels are lowercase.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Functions to excecute when a source is disconnected
* <code>password</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"hackme"</code>): Source password.
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>8005</code>): Port used to connect to the source.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Replay last known metadata when switching back to this source. This helps when source has dropped due to temporary connection issues.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for source connectionn.
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"source"</code>): Source user.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Mountpoint to look for.

h5@input_harbor_ssl. input.harbor.ssl
<pre>(?id:string,?auth:((string,string)->bool),?buffer:float,
 ?debug:bool,?dumpfile:string,?icy:bool,
 ?icy_metadata_charset:string,?logfile:string,?max:float,
 ?metadata_charset:string,
 ?on_connect:(([(string*string)])->unit),
 ?on_disconnect:(()->unit),?password:string,?port:int,
 ?replay_metadata:bool,?timeout:float,?user:string,
 string)->source('a)</pre>

Retrieves the given https stream from the harbor.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>auth</code> (<code>(string,string)->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_,_) -> false</code>): Authentication function. <code>f(login,password)</code> returns <code>true</code> if the user should be granted access for this login. Override any other method if used.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>debug</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Run in debugging mode by not catching some exceptions.
* <code>dumpfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Dump stream to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>icy</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Enable ICY (shoutcast) protocol.
* <code>icy_metadata_charset</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): ICY (shoutcast) metadata charset. Guessed if empty. Default for shoutcast is ISO-8859-1. Set to that value if all your clients send metadata using this charset and automatic detection is not working for you.
* <code>logfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Log buffer status to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>metadata_charset</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Metadata charset for non-ICY (shoutcast) source protocols. Guessed if empty.
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): Function to execute when a source is connected. Its receives the list of headers, of the form: (<label>,<value>). All labels are lowercase.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Functions to excecute when a source is disconnected
* <code>password</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"hackme"</code>): Source password.
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>8005</code>): Port used to connect to the source.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Replay last known metadata when switching back to this source. This helps when source has dropped due to temporary connection issues.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for source connectionn.
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"source"</code>): Source user.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Mountpoint to look for.

h5@input_http. input.http
<pre>(?id:string,?autostart:bool,?bind_address:string,
 ?buffer:float,?debug:bool,?force_mime:string,
 ?logfile:string,?max:float,?new_track_on_metadata:bool,
 ?on_connect:(([(string*string)])->unit),
 ?on_disconnect:(()->unit),?playlist_mode:string,
 ?poll_delay:float,?timeout:float,?user_agent:string,
 string)->source('a)</pre>

Forwards the given http stream. The relay can be paused/resumed using the start/stop telnet commands.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>autostart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Initially start relaying or not.
* <code>bind_address</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Address to bind on the local machine. This option can be useful if your machine is bound to multiple IPs. Empty means no bind address.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>debug</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Run in debugging mode, not catching some exceptions.
* <code>force_mime</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force mime data type. Not used if empty.
* <code>logfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Log buffer status to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>new_track_on_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Treat new metadata as new track.
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): Function to execute when a source is connected. Its receives the list of headers, of the form: (<label>,<value>). All labels are lowercase.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Function to excecute when a source is disconnected
* <code>playlist_mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"normal"</code>): Valid modes are "normal", "random", "randomize" and "first". The first ones have the same meaning as for the mode parameter of the playlist operator. The last one discards all entries but the first one.
* <code>poll_delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Polling delay when trying to connect to the stream.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for source connectionn.
* <code>user_agent</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Liquidsoap/1.3.0+scm (Unix; OCaml 4.04.0)"</code>): User agent.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URL of an http stream (default port is 80).

h5@input_https. input.https
<pre>(?id:string,?autostart:bool,?bind_address:string,
 ?buffer:float,?debug:bool,?force_mime:string,
 ?logfile:string,?max:float,?new_track_on_metadata:bool,
 ?on_connect:(([(string*string)])->unit),
 ?on_disconnect:(()->unit),?playlist_mode:string,
 ?poll_delay:float,?timeout:float,?user_agent:string,
 string)->source('a)</pre>

Forwards the given https stream. The relay can be paused/resumed using the start/stop telnet commands.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>autostart</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Initially start relaying or not.
* <code>bind_address</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Address to bind on the local machine. This option can be useful if your machine is bound to multiple IPs. Empty means no bind address.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Duration of the pre-buffered data.
* <code>debug</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Run in debugging mode, not catching some exceptions.
* <code>force_mime</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force mime data type. Not used if empty.
* <code>logfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Log buffer status to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum duration of the buffered data.
* <code>new_track_on_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Treat new metadata as new track.
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): Function to execute when a source is connected. Its receives the list of headers, of the form: (<label>,<value>). All labels are lowercase.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Function to excecute when a source is disconnected
* <code>playlist_mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"normal"</code>): Valid modes are "normal", "random", "randomize" and "first". The first ones have the same meaning as for the mode parameter of the playlist operator. The last one discards all entries but the first one.
* <code>poll_delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Polling delay when trying to connect to the stream.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for source connectionn.
* <code>user_agent</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Liquidsoap/1.3.0+scm (Unix; OCaml 4.04.0)"</code>): User agent.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URL of an https stream (default port is 80).

h5@playlist. playlist
<pre>(?id:string,?check_next:((request('a))->bool),
 ?conservative:bool,?default_duration:float,
 ?length:float,?mime_type:string,?mode:string,
 ?prefix:string,?reload:int,?reload_mode:string,
 ?timeout:float,string)->source('a)</pre>

Loop on a playlist of URIs.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>check_next</code> (<code>(request('a))->bool</code> -- defaults to <code><fun></code>): Function used to filter next tracks. A candidate track is only validated if the function returns true on it. The function is called before resolution, hence metadata will only be available for requests corresponding to local files. This is typically used to avoid repetitions, but be careful: if the function rejects all attempts, the playlist will enter into a consuming loop and stop playing anything.
* <code>conservative</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): If true, estimated remaining time on the current track is not considered when computing queue length.
* <code>default_duration</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): When unknown, assume this duration (in sec.) for files.
* <code>length</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): How much audio (in sec.) should be queued in advance.
* <code>mime_type</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Default MIME type for the playlist. Empty string means automatic detection.
* <code>mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"randomize"</code>): Play the files in the playlist either in the order ("normal" mode), or shuffle the playlist each time it is loaded, and play it in this order for a whole round ("randomize" mode), or pick a random file in the playlist each time ("random" mode).
* <code>prefix</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Add a constant prefix to all requests. Useful for passing extra information using annotate, or for resolution through a particular protocol, such as replaygain.
* <code>reload</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>0</code>): Amount of time (in seconds or rounds), when applicable, before which the playlist is reloaded; 0 means never.
* <code>reload_mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"seconds"</code>): Unit of the reload parameter, either 'rounds', 'seconds' or 'watch' (reload the file whenever it is changed).
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>20.0</code>): Timeout (in sec.) for a single download.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URI where to find the playlist.

h5@playlist_once. playlist.once
<pre>(?id:string,?random:bool,?on_done:(()->unit),
 ?reload_mode:string,string)->source('a)</pre>

Custom playlist source written using the script language. It will read directory or playlist, play all files and stop.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>random</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Randomize playlist content
* <code>on_done</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Function to execute when the playlist is finished
* <code>reload_mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): If set to "watch", will be reloaded when the playlist is changed
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Playlist URI

h5@playlist_reloadable. playlist.reloadable
<pre>(?id:string,?random:bool,?on_done:(()->unit),
 ?filter:(([(string*string)])->bool),string)->
(((?uri:string)->unit)*source('a))</pre>

Custom playlist source written using the script language.  Will read directory or playlist, play all files and stop.  Returns a pair @(reload,source)@ where @reload@ is a function of type @(?uri:string)->unit@ used to reload the source and @source@ is the actual source. The reload function can optionally be called with a new playlist URI. Otherwise, it reloads the previous URI.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>random</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Randomize playlist content
* <code>on_done</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Function to execute when the playlist is finished
* <code>filter</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> true</code>): Filter out some files depending on metadata
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Playlist URI

h5@playlist_safe. playlist.safe
<pre>(?id:string,?mime_type:string,?mode:string,
 ?prefix:string,?reload:int,?reload_mode:string,string)->
source('a)</pre>

Loop on a playlist of local files, and never fail. In order to do so, it has to check every file at the loading, so the streamer startup may take a few seconds. To avoid this, use a standard playlist, and put only a few local files in a default safe_playlist in order to ensure the liveness of the streamer.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>mime_type</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Default MIME type for the playlist. Empty string means automatic detection.
* <code>mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"randomize"</code>): Play the files in the playlist either in the order ("normal" mode), or shuffle the playlist each time it is loaded, and play it in this order for a whole round ("randomize" mode), or pick a random file in the playlist each time ("random" mode).
* <code>prefix</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Add a constant prefix to all requests. Useful for passing extra information using annotate, or for resolution through a particular protocol, such as replaygain.
* <code>reload</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>0</code>): Amount of time (in seconds or rounds), when applicable, before which the playlist is reloaded; 0 means never.
* <code>reload_mode</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"seconds"</code>): Unit of the reload parameter, either 'rounds', 'seconds' or 'watch' (reload the file whenever it is changed).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URI where to find the playlist.

h3@Source___Liquidsoap. Source / Liquidsoap
h5@buffer. buffer
<pre>(?id:string,?buffer:float,?fallible:bool,?max:float,
 ?on_start:(()->unit),?on_stop:(()->unit),?start:bool,
 source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Create a buffer between two different clocks.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Amount of data to pre-buffer, in seconds.
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum amount of buffered data, in seconds.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@buffer_adaptative. buffer.adaptative
<pre>(?id:string,?averaging:float,?buffer:float,
 ?fallible:bool,?limit:float,?max:float,
 ?on_start:(()->unit),?on_stop:(()->unit),?reset:bool,
 ?start:bool,source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>
WARNING: This is only EXPERIMENTAL!

Create a buffer between two different clocks. The speed of the output is adapted so that no buffer underrun or overrun occurs. This wonderful behavior has a cost: the pitch of the sound might be changed a little.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>averaging</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Half-life for the averaging of the buffer size, in seconds.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Amount of data to pre-buffer, in seconds.
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>limit</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.25</code>): Maximum acceleration or deceleration factor.
* <code>max</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>10.0</code>): Maximum amount of buffered data, in seconds.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>reset</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Reset speed estimation to 1. when the source becomes available again.
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>)

Encode an x264 video file using gstreamer

h5@gstreamer_rtp_mpeg4. gstreamer.rtp.mpeg4
<pre>(?host:string,?port:int,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b+1,midi='#c))->
active_source(audio='#a,video='#b+1,midi='#c)</pre>

Broadcast a video in RTP. In order to play it, save the following in xxx.sdp and use vlc xxx.sdp: v=0 m=video 5000 RTP/AVP 96 c=IN IP4 127.0.0.1 a=rtpmap:96 MP4V-ES/90000

* <code>host</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"127.0.0.1"</code>)
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>5000</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b+1,midi='#c)</code>)

Output stream to local sound card using libao.

* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>options</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): List of parameters, depends on the driver.
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.

If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@output_file. output.file
<pre>(?id:string,?append:bool,?dir_perm:int,?fallible:bool,
 ?flush:bool,?on_close:((string)->unit),
 ?on_start:(()->unit),?on_stop:(()->unit),?perm:int,
 ?reopen_delay:float,?reopen_on_metadata:bool,
 ?reopen_when:(()->bool),?start:bool,format('a),string,
 source('a))->active_source('a)</pre>

Output the source stream to a file.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>append</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Do not truncate but append in the file if it exists.
* <code>dir_perm</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>511</code>): Permission of the directories if some have to be created, up to umask. Although you can enter values in octal notation (0oXXX) they will be displayed in decimal (for instance, 0o777 = 7*8^2 + 7*8 + 7 = 511).
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>flush</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Perform a flush after each write.
* <code>on_close</code> (<code>(string)->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): This function will be called for each file, after that it is finished and closed. The filename will be passed as argument.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>perm</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>438</code>): Permission of the file if it has to be created, up to umask. You can and should write this number in octal notation: 0oXXX. The default value is however displayed in decimal (0o666 = 6*8^2 + 6*8 + 6 = 438).
* <code>reopen_delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>120.0</code>): Prevent re-opening within that delay, in seconds.
* <code>reopen_on_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Re-open on every new metadata information.
* <code>reopen_when</code> (<code>()->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>{false}</code>): When should the output be re-opened.
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>format('a)</code>): Encoding format.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Filename where to output the stream. Some strftime conversion specifiers are available: <code>%SMHdmY</code>. You can also use <code>$(..)</code> interpolation notation for metadata.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@output_harbor. output.harbor
<pre>(?id:string,?auth:((string,string)->bool),?buffer:int,
 ?burst:int,?chunk:int,?dumpfile:string,?encoding:string,
 ?fallible:bool,?format:string,
 ?headers:[(string*string)],?metaint:int,mount:string,
 ?on_connect:((headers:[(string*string)],uri:string,
               protocol:string,string)->unit),
 ?on_disconnect:((string)->unit),?on_start:(()->unit),
 ?on_stop:(()->unit),?password:string,?port:int,
 ?start:bool,?timeout:float,?url:string,?user:string,
 format('a),source('a))->active_source('a)</pre>

Encode and output the stream using the harbor server.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>auth</code> (<code>(string,string)->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_,_) -> false</code>): Authentication function. <code>f(login,password)</code> returns <code>true</code> if the user should be granted access for this login. Override any other method if used.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>327675</code>): Maximun buffer per-client.
* <code>burst</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>65534</code>): Initial burst of data sent to the client.
* <code>chunk</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>1024</code>): Send data to clients using chunks of at least this length.
* <code>dumpfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Dump stream to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>encoding</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Encoding used to send metadata. If empty, defaults to "ISO-8859-1" for non-ogg formats and "UTF-8" otherwise.
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>format</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Format, e.g. "audio/ogg". When empty, the encoder is used to guess.
* <code>headers</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Additional headers.
* <code>metaint</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>16000</code>): Interval used to send ICY metadata
* <code>mount</code> (<code>string</code>)
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>(headers:[(string*string)],uri:string,protocol:string,
 string)->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (~headers,~uri,~protocol,_) -> ()</code>): Callback executed when connection is established.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>(string)->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> ()</code>): Callback executed when connection stops.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>password</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"hackme"</code>)
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>8000</code>)
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for network operations.
* <code>url</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): User for client connection, disabled if empty.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>format('a)</code>): Encoding format.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@output_icecast. output.icecast
<pre>(?id:string,?chunked:bool,?connection_timeout:float,
 ?description:string,?dumpfile:string,?encoding:string,
 ?fallible:bool,?format:string,?genre:string,
 ?headers:[(string*string)],?host:string,?icy_id:int,
 ?icy_metadata:string,?mount:string,?name:string,
 ?on_connect:(()->unit),?on_disconnect:(()->unit),
 ?on_error:((string)->float),?on_start:(()->unit),
 ?on_stop:(()->unit),?password:string,?port:int,
 ?protocol:string,?public:bool,?start:bool,
 ?timeout:float,?url:string,?user:string,?verb:string,
 format('a),source('a))->active_source('a)</pre>

Encode and output the stream to an icecast2 or shoutcast server.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>chunked</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Used cunked transfer with the 'http(s)' protocol.
* <code>connection_timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Timeout for establishing network connections (disabled is negative).
* <code>description</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>dumpfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Dump stream to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>encoding</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Encoding used to send metadata. If empty, defaults to "UTF-8" for "http(s)" protocol and "ISO-8859-1" for "icy" protocol.
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>format</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Format, e.g. "audio/ogg". When empty, the encoder is used to guess.
* <code>genre</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>headers</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[("User-Agent","Liquidsoap/1.3.0+scm (Unix; OCaml 4.04.0)")]</code>): Additional headers.
* <code>host</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"localhost"</code>)
* <code>icy_id</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>1</code>): Shoutcast source ID. Only supported by Shoutcast v2.
* <code>icy_metadata</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"guess"</code>): Send new metadata using the ICY protocol. One of: "guess", "true", "false"
* <code>mount</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Use [name]"</code>): Source mount point. Mandatory when streaming to icecast.
* <code>name</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Use [mount]"</code>)
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when connection is established.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when connection stops.
* <code>on_error</code> (<code>(string)->float</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> 3.</code>): Callback executed when an error happens. The callback receives a string representation of the error that occured and returns a float. If returned value is positive, connection will be tried again after this amount of time (in seconds).
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>password</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"hackme"</code>)
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>8000</code>)
* <code>protocol</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"http"</code>): Protocol of the streaming server: 'http' or 'https' for Icecast, 'icy' for shoutcast.
* <code>public</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Timeout for network read and write.
* <code>url</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): User for shout source connection. Defaults to "source" for icecast connections. Useful only in special cases, like with per-mountpoint users.
* <code>verb</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"source"</code>): Verb to use with the 'http(s)' protocol. One of: 'source', 'put' or 'post'.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>format('a)</code>): Encoding format.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@output_portaudio. output.portaudio
<pre>(?id:string,?buflen:int,?clock_safe:bool,?fallible:bool,
 ?on_start:(()->unit),?on_stop:(()->unit),?start:bool,
 source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c))->
active_source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Output the source's stream to a portaudio output device.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>buflen</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>256</code>): Length of a buffer in samples.
* <code>clock_safe</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Force the use of the dedicated Portaudio clock.
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Automatically start outputting whenever possible. If true, an infallible (normal) output will start outputting as soon as it is created, and a fallible output will (re)start as soon as its source becomes available for streaming.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@output_prefered. output.prefered
<pre>(?id:string,?fallible:bool,?on_start:(()->unit),
 ?on_stop:(()->unit),?start:bool,
 source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c))->
active_source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>)
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>)
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@output_shoutcast. output.shoutcast
<pre>(?id:string,?start:bool,?host:string,?port:int,
 ?user:string,?password:string,?genre:string,?url:string,
 ?name:string,?public:bool,?icy_id:int,?format:string,
 ?dj:(()->string),?dumpfile:string,?icy_metadata:string,
 ?on_connect:(()->unit),?on_disconnect:(()->unit),
 ?aim:string,?icq:string,?irc:string,?icy_reset:bool,
 ?fallible:bool,?on_start:(()->unit),?on_stop:(()->unit),
 ?on_error:((string)->float),format('a),source('a))->
active_source('a)</pre>

Output to shoutcast.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"output.shoutcast"</code>): Output's ID
* <code>start</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Start output threads on operator initialization.
* <code>host</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"localhost"</code>)
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>8000</code>)
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): User for shout source connection. Useful only in special cases, like with per-mountpoint users.
* <code>password</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"hackme"</code>)
* <code>genre</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>url</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>name</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>public</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>icy_id</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>1</code>): Shoutcast source ID. Only supported by Shoutcast v2.
* <code>format</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Format, e.g. "audio/ogg". When empty, the encoder is used to guess.
* <code>dj</code> (<code>()->string</code> -- defaults to <code>{""}</code>): Callback to set dj name.
* <code>dumpfile</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Dump stream to file, for debugging purpose. Disabled if empty.
* <code>icy_metadata</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"guess"</code>): Send new metadata using the ICY protocol. One of: "guess", "true", "false"
* <code>on_connect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when connection starts.
* <code>on_disconnect</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when connection stops.
* <code>aim</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>icq</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>irc</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>icy_reset</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Reset shoutcast source buffer upon connecting (necessary for NSV).
* <code>fallible</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Allow the child source to fail, in which case the output will be (temporarily) stopped.
* <code>on_start</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting starts.
* <code>on_stop</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Callback executed when outputting stops.
* <code>on_error</code> (<code>(string)->float</code> -- defaults to <code>fun (_) -> 3.</code>): Callback executed when an error happens. If returned value is positive, connection wll be tried again after this amount of time (in seconds).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>format('a)</code>): Encoding format. For shoutcast, should be mp3 or AAC(+).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>): The source to output

h3@Source___Sound_Processing. Source / Sound Processing
h5@add. add
<pre>(?id:string,?normalize:bool,?weights:[int],
 [source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)])->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

Mix sources, with optional normalization. Only relay metadata from the first source that is effectively summed.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>normalize</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>)
* <code>weights</code> (<code>[int]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Relative weight of the sources in the sum. The empty list stands for the homogeneous distribution.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)]</code>)

h5@amplify. amplify
<pre>(?id:string,?override:string,'a,
 source(audio='#b,video='#c,midi='#d))->
source(audio='#b,video='#c,midi='#d)
where 'a is either float or ()->float</pre>

Multiply the amplitude of the signal.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>override</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_amplify"</code>): Specify the name of a metadata field that, when present and well-formed, overrides the amplification factor for the current track. Well-formed values are floats in decimal notation (e.g. '0.7') which are taken as normal/linear multiplicative factors; values can be passed in decibels with the suffix 'dB' (e.g. '-8.2 dB', but the spaces do not matter).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code>): Multiplicative factor.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#b,video='#c,midi='#d)</code>)

h5@comb. comb

where 'a is either float or ()->float</pre>

* <code>delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.001</code>): Delay in seconds.

h5@compress. compress
<pre>(?id:string,?attack:'a,?gain:'b,?knee:'c,?ratio:float,
 ?release:'d,?rms_window:float,?threshold:'e,
 source(audio='#f,video='#g,midi='#h))->
source(audio='#f,video='#g,midi='#h)
where 'a, 'b, 'c, 'd, 'e is either float or ()->float</pre>

Compress the signal.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>attack</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>100.0</code>): Attack time (ms).
* <code>gain</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Additional gain (dB).
* <code>knee</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Knee radius (dB).
* <code>ratio</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Gain reduction ratio (n:1).
* <code>release</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>400.0</code>): Release time (ms).
* <code>rms_window</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.1</code>): Window for computing RMS (in sec).
* <code>threshold</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>-10.0</code>): Threshold level (dB).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#f,video='#g,midi='#h)</code>)

h5@compress_exponential. compress.exponential
<pre>(?id:string,?mu:float,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Exponential compressor.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>mu</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Exponential compression factor, typically greater than 1.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@cross. cross
<pre>(?id:string,?active:bool,?conservative:bool,
 ?duration:float,?inhibit:float,?minimum:float,
 ?override:string,((source('a),source('a))->source('a)),
 source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Generic cross operator, allowing the composition of the N last seconds of a track with the beginning of the next track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>active</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): The active behavior is to keep ticking the child's clock when the operator is not streaming. Otherwise the child's clock is strictly based on what is streamed off the child source, which results in time-dependent active sources to be frozen when that source is stopped.
* <code>conservative</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Do not trust remaining time estimations, always buffering data in advance. This avoids being tricked by skips, either manual or caused by skip_blank().
* <code>duration</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Duration in seconds of the crossed end of track. This value can be changed on a per-file basis using a special metadata field.
* <code>inhibit</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Minimum delay between two transitions. It is useful in order to avoid that a transition is triggered on top of another when an end-of-track occurs in the first one. Negative values mean <code>duration+1</code>. Warning: zero inhibition can cause infinite loops.
* <code>minimum</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Minimum duration (in sec.) for a cross: If the track ends without any warning (e.g. in case of skip) there may not be enough data for a decent composition. Set to 0. to avoid having transitions after skips, or more to avoid transitions on short tracks. With the negative default, transitions always occur.
* <code>override</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_start_next"</code>): Metadata field which, if present and containing a float, overrides the 'duration' parameter for current track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(source('a),source('a))->source('a)</code>): Composition of an end of track and the next track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@echo. echo
<pre>(?id:string,?delay:'a,?feedback:'b,?ping_pong:bool,
 source(audio='#c,video='#d,midi='#e))->

where 'a, 'b is either float or ()->float</pre>

Add echo.

* <code>delay</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.5</code>): Delay in seconds.
* <code>feedback</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>-6.0</code>): Feedback coefficient in dB (negative).
* <code>ping_pong</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Use ping-pong delay.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#c,video='#d,midi='#e)</code>)

h5@fade_final. fade.final
<pre>(?id:string,?duration:float,?override_duration:string,

* <code>duration</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>3.0</code>): Duration of the fading. This value can be set on a per-file basis using the metadata field passed as override.
* <code>override_duration</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_fade_final"</code>): Metadata field which, if present and containing a float, overrides the 'duration' parameter for current track.
* <code>override_type</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_fade_type"</code>): Metadata field which, if present and correct, overrides the 'type' parameter for current track.
* <code>type</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"lin"</code>): Fader shape (lin|sin|log|exp): linear, sinusoidal, logarithmic or exponential.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@filter. filter
<pre>(?id:string,freq:'a,mode:string,?q:'b,?wetness:'c,
 source(audio='#d,video='#e,midi='#f))->
source(audio='#d,video='#e,midi='#f)
where 'a, 'b, 'c is either float or ()->float</pre>

Perform several kinds of filtering on the signal

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>freq</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code>)
* <code>mode</code> (<code>string</code>): Available modes are 'low' (for low-pass filter), 'high' (for high-pass filter), 'band' (for band-pass filter) and 'notch' (for notch / band-stop / band-rejection filter).
* <code>q</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>)
* <code>wetness</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): How much of the original signal should be added (1. means only filtered and 0. means only original signal).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#d,video='#e,midi='#f)</code>)

h5@filter_fir. filter.fir
<pre>(?id:string,beta:float,?coeffs:int,frequency:float,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Low-pass FIR filter.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>beta</code> (<code>float</code>): Beta should range between 0 and 1.
* <code>coeffs</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>255</code>): Number of coefficients
* <code>frequency</code> (<code>float</code>): Corner frequency in Hz (frequency at which the response is 0.5, that is -6 dB).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@filter_iir_butterworth_bandpass. filter.iir.butterworth.bandpass
<pre>(?id:string,frequency1:float,frequency2:float,?order:int,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

IIR filter

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>frequency1</code> (<code>float</code>): First corner frequency

h5@normalize. normalize
<pre>(?id:string,?gain_max:'a,?gain_min:'b,?k_down:'c,
 ?k_up:'d,?target:'e,?threshold:'f,?window:float,
 source(audio='#g,video='#h,midi='#i))->
source(audio='#g,video='#h,midi='#i)
where 'a, 'b, 'c, 'd, 'e, 'f is either float or ()->float</pre>

Normalize the signal. Dynamic normalization of the signal is sometimes the only option, and can make a listening experience much nicer. However, its dynamic aspect implies some limitations which can go as far as creating saturation in some extreme cases. If possible, consider using some track-based normalization techniques such as those based on replay gain. See the documentation for more details.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>gain_max</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>6.0</code>): Maximal gain value (dB).
* <code>gain_min</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>-6.0</code>): Minimal gain value (dB).
* <code>k_down</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.1</code>): Coefficient when the power must go down (between 0 and 1, slowest to fastest).
* <code>k_up</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.005</code>): Coefficient when the power must go up (between 0 and 1, slowest to fastest).
* <code>target</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>-13.0</code>): Desired RMS (dB).
* <code>threshold</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>-40.0</code>): Minimal RMS for activaing gain control (dB).
* <code>window</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.1</code>): Duration of the window used to compute the current RMS power (second).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#g,video='#h,midi='#i)</code>)

h5@smart_cross. smart_cross
<pre>(?id:string,?active:bool,?conservative:bool,
 ?duration:float,?inhibit:float,?minimum:float,
 ?width:float,
 ((float,float,[(string*string)],[(string*string)],
   source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0),
   source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
  source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)),
 source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Cross operator, allowing the composition of the N last seconds of a track with the beginning of the next track, using a transition function depending on the relative power of the signal before and after the end of track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>active</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): The active behavior is to keep ticking the child's clock when the operator is not streaming. Otherwise the child's clock is strictly based on what is streamed off the child source, which results in time-dependent active sources to be frozen when that source is stopped.
* <code>conservative</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Do not trust remaining time estimations, always buffering data in advance. This avoids being tricked by skips, either manual or caused by skip_blank().
* <code>duration</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Duration in seconds of the crossed end of track.
* <code>inhibit</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Minimum delay between two transitions. It is useful in order to avoid that a transition is triggered on top of another when an end-of-track occurs in the first one. Negative values mean <code>duration+1</code>. Warning: zero inhibition can cause infinite loops.
* <code>minimum</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Minimum duration (in sec.) for a cross: If the track ends without any warning (e.g. in case of skip) there may not be enough data for a decent composition. Set to 0. to avoid having transitions after skips, or more to avoid transitions on short tracks. With the negative default, transitions always occur.
* <code>width</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Width of the power computation window.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(float,float,[(string*string)],[(string*string)],
 source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0),
 source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>): Transition function, composing from the end of a track and the next track. It also takes the power of the signal before and after the transition, and the metadata.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>)

* <code>pan</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Pan ranges between -1 and 1.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio=2,video=0,midi=0)</code>)

h5@stretch. stretch
<pre>(?id:string,?active:bool,ratio:'a,
 source(audio='#b+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#c+1,video=0,midi=0)
where 'a is either float or ()->float</pre>

Slow down or accelerate an audio stream by stretching (sounds lower) or squeezing it (sounds higher).

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>active</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): The active behavior is to keep ticking the child's clock when the operator is not streaming. Otherwise the child's clock is strictly based on what is streamed off the child source, which results in time-dependent active sources to be frozen when that source is stopped.
* <code>ratio</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code>): A value higher than 1 means slowing down.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#b+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>)



h3@Source___Sound_Synthesis. Source / Sound Synthesis
h5@synth_all_saw. synth.all.saw
<pre>(?id:string,?attack:float,?decay:float,?envelope:bool,
 ?release:float,?sustain:float,
 source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c+16))->
source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c+16)</pre>

Saw synthesizer. It creates one synthesizer for each channel.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>attack</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.02</code>): Envelope attack (in seconds).
* <code>decay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.01</code>): Envelope decay (in seconds).
* <code>envelope</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Use envelope.
* <code>release</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.01</code>): Envelope release (in seconds).
* <code>sustain</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.9</code>): Envelope sustain level.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c+16)</code>)

h5@synth_all_sine. synth.all.sine
<pre>(?id:string,?attack:float,?decay:float,?envelope:bool,
 ?release:float,?sustain:float,
 source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c+16))->
source(audio='#a+1,video='#b,midi='#c+16)</pre>

Sine synthesizer. It creates one synthesizer for each channel.
