h3@Source___Track_Processing. Source / Track Processing
h5@append. append
<pre>(?id:string,?insert_missing:bool,?merge:bool,source('a),
 (([(string*string)])->source('a)))->source('a)</pre>

Append an extra track to every track. Set the metadata 'liq_append' to 'false' to inhibit appending on one track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>insert_missing</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Treat track beginnings without metadata as having empty one.
* <code>merge</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Merge the track with its appended track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->source('a)</code>): Given the metadata, build the source producing the track to append. This source is allowed to fail (produce nothing) if no relevant track is to be appended.

h5@at. at
<pre>((()->bool),source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Restrict a source to play only when a predicate is true.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>()->bool</code>): The predicate, typically a time interval such as <code>{10h-10h30}</code>.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@crossfade. crossfade
<pre>(?id:string,?conservative:bool,?start_next:float,
 ?fade_in:float,?fade_out:float,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

Simple crossfade.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>conservative</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Always prepare for a premature end-of-track.
* <code>start_next</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Duration in seconds of the crossed end of track.
* <code>fade_in</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>3.0</code>): Duration of the fade in for next track.
* <code>fade_out</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>3.0</code>): Duration of the fade out for previous track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</code>): The source to use.

h5@cue_cut. cue_cut
<pre>(?id:string,?cue_in_metadata:string,
 ?cue_out_metadata:string,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Start track after a cue in point and stop it at cue out point. The cue points are given as metadata, in seconds from the begining of tracks.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>cue_in_metadata</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_cue_in"</code>): Metadata for cue in points.
* <code>cue_out_metadata</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_cue_out"</code>): Metadata for cue out points.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@delay. delay
<pre>(?id:string,?initial:bool,float,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Prevents the child from being ready again too fast after a end of track

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>initial</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Start in unavailable state, as if a track had just finished.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>float</code>): The source won't be ready less than this amount of seconds after any end of track
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@drop_metadata. drop_metadata
<pre>(source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Removes all metadata coming from a source.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@eat_blank. eat_blank
<pre>(?id:string,?at_beginning:bool,?max_blank:float,
 ?min_noise:float,?start_blank:bool,?threshold:float,
 ?track_sensitive:bool,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Eat blanks, i.e., drop the contents of the stream until it is not blank anymore.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>at_beginning</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Only eat at the beginning of a track.
* <code>max_blank</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>20.0</code>): Maximum duration of silence allowed, in seconds.
* <code>min_noise</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Minimum duration of noise required to end silence, in seconds.
* <code>start_blank</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Start assuming we have blank.
* <code>threshold</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-40.0</code>): Power in decibels under which the stream is considered silent.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Reset blank counter at each track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@fallback. fallback
<pre>(?id:string,?replay_metadata:bool,?track_sensitive:'a,
 ?transitions:[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)],
 [source('b)])->source('b)
where 'a is either bool or ()->bool</pre>

At the beginning of each track, select the first ready child.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Replay the last metadata of a child when switching to it in the middle of a track.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>anything that is either bool or ()->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Re-select only on end of tracks.
* <code>transitions</code> (<code>[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Transition functions, padded with <code>fun (x,y) -> y</code> functions.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('b)]</code>): Select the first ready source in this list.

h5@fallback_skip. fallback.skip
<pre>(input:source('a),source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Special track insensitive fallback that always skips current song before switching.

* <code>input</code> (<code>source('a)</code>): The input source
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>): The fallback source

h5@insert_metadata. insert_metadata
<pre>(?id:string,source('a))->
((([(string*string)])->unit)*source('a))</pre>

Dynamically insert metadata in a stream. Returns a pair (f,s) where s is a new source and f is a function of type (metadata)->unit, used to insert metadata in s.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@map_metadata. map_metadata
<pre>(?id:string,?insert_missing:bool,?strip:bool,
 ?update:bool,(([(string*string)])->[(string*string)]),
 source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Rewrite metadata on the fly using a function.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>insert_missing</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Treat track beginnings without metadata as having empty ones. The operational order is: create empty if needed, map and strip if enabled.
* <code>strip</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Completely remove empty metadata. Operates on both empty values and empty metadata chunk.
* <code>update</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Only update metadata. If false, only returned values will be set as metadata.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->[(string*string)]</code>): A function that returns new metadata.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@merge_tracks. merge_tracks
<pre>(?id:string,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Merge consecutive tracks from the input source.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@mksafe. mksafe
<pre>(?id:string,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Turn a source into an infaillible source by adding blank when the source is not available.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"mksafe"</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>): the source to turn infaillible

h5@notify_metadata. notify_metadata
<pre>(?urgency:string,?icon:string,?time:int,
 ?display:(([(string*string)])->string),?title:string,
 source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Use notify to display metadata info.

* <code>urgency</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"low"</code>): Urgency (low|normal|critical).
* <code>icon</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"stock_smiley-22"</code>): Icon filename or stock icon to display.
* <code>time</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>3000</code>): Timeout in milliseconds.
* <code>display</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->string</code> -- defaults to <code><fun></code>): Function used to display a metadata packet.
* <code>title</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Liquidsoap: new track"</code>): Title of the notification message.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@on_blank. on_blank
<pre>(?id:string,?max_blank:float,?min_noise:float,
 ?on_noise:(()->unit),?start_blank:bool,?threshold:float,
 ?track_sensitive:bool,(()->unit),
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Calls a given handler when detecting a blank.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>max_blank</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>20.0</code>): Maximum duration of silence allowed, in seconds.
* <code>min_noise</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Minimum duration of noise required to end silence, in seconds.
* <code>on_noise</code> (<code>()->unit</code> -- defaults to <code>{()}</code>): Handler called when noise is detected.
* <code>start_blank</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Start assuming we have blank.
* <code>threshold</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-40.0</code>): Power in decibels under which the stream is considered silent.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Reset blank counter at each track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>()->unit</code>): Handler called when blank is detected.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@on_end. on_end
<pre>(?id:string,?delay:float,
 ((float,[(string*string)])->unit),source('a))->
source('a)</pre>

Call a given handler when there is less than a given amount of time remaining before then end of track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Execute handler when remaining time is less or equal to this value.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(float,[(string*string)])->unit</code>): Function to execute. First argument is the remaining time, second is the latest metadata. That function should be fast because it is executed in the main streaming thread.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@on_metadata. on_metadata
<pre>(?id:string,(([(string*string)])->unit),source('a))->
source('a)</pre>

Call a given handler on metadata packets.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code>): Function called on every metadata packet in the stream. It should be fast because it is executed in the main streaming thread.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@on_offset. on_offset
<pre>(?id:string,?force:bool,?offset:float,?override:string,
 ((float,[(string*string)])->unit),source('a))->
source('a)</pre>

Call a given handler when position in track is equal or more than a given amount of time.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>force</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Force execution of callback if track ends before 'offset' position has been reached.
* <code>offset</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Execute handler when position in track is equal or more than to this value.
* <code>override</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_on_offset"</code>): Metadata field which, if present and containing a float, overrides the 'offset' parameter.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(float,[(string*string)])->unit</code>): Function to execute. First argument is the actual position within the current track, second is the latest metadata. That function should be fast because it is executed in the main streaming thread.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@on_track. on_track
<pre>(?id:string,(([(string*string)])->unit),source('a))->
source('a)</pre>

Call a given handler on new tracks.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->unit</code>): Function called on every beginning of track in the stream, with the corresponding metadata as argument. If there is no metadata at the beginning of track, the empty list is passed. That function should be fast because it is executed in the main streaming thread.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@once. once
<pre>(source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Creates a source that plays only one track of the input source.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>): The input source.

h5@osd_metadata. osd_metadata
<pre>(?color:string,?position:string,?font:string,
 ?display:(([(string*string)])->string),source('a))->
source('a)</pre>

Use X On Screen Display to display metadata info.

* <code>color</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"green"</code>): Color of the text.
* <code>position</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"top"</code>): Position of the text (top|middle|bottom).
* <code>font</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"-*-courier-*-r-*-*-*-240-*-*-*-*-*-*"</code>): Font used (xfontsel is your friend...)
* <code>display</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->string</code> -- defaults to <code><fun></code>): Function used to display a metadata packet.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@overlap_sources. overlap_sources
<pre>(?id:string,?normalize:bool,?start_next:string,
 ?weights:[int],[source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)])->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

Rotate between overlapping sources. Next track starts according to 'liq_start_next' offset metadata.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>normalize</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>)
* <code>start_next</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"liq_start_next"</code>): Metadata field indicating when the next track should start, relative to current track's time.
* <code>weights</code> (<code>[int]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Relative weight of the sources in the sum. The empty list stands for the homogeneous distribution.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)]</code>): Sources to toggle from

h5@playlist_merge. playlist.merge
<pre>(?id:string,?random:bool,string)->source('a)</pre>

Play the whole playlist as one track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>random</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Randomize playlist content
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Playlist URI.

h5@prepend. prepend
<pre>(?id:string,?merge:bool,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c),
 (([(string*string)])->
  source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Prepend an extra track before every track. Set the metadata 'liq_prepend' to 'false' to inhibit prepending on one track.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>merge</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Merge the track with its appended track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>([(string*string)])->source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>): Given the metadata, build the source producing the track to prepend. This source is allowed to fail (produce nothing) if no relevant track is to be appended. However, success must be immediate or it will not be taken into account.

h5@random. random
<pre>(?id:string,?replay_metadata:bool,?track_sensitive:'a,
 ?transitions:[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)],
 ?weights:[int],[source('b)])->source('b)
where 'a is either bool or ()->bool</pre>

At the beginning of every track, select a random ready child.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Replay the last metadata of a child when switching to it in the middle of a track.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>anything that is either bool or ()->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Re-select only on end of tracks.
* <code>transitions</code> (<code>[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Transition functions, padded with <code>fun (x,y) -> y</code> functions.
* <code>weights</code> (<code>[int]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Weights of the children (padded with 1), defining for each child the probability that it is selected.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('b)]</code>)

h5@rewrite_metadata. rewrite_metadata
<pre>([(string*string)],?insert_missing:bool,?update:bool,
 ?strip:bool,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Rewrite metadata on the fly using a list of (target,rules).

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code>): List of (target,value) rewriting rules.
* <code>insert_missing</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Treat track beginnings without metadata as having empty ones. The operational order is: create empty if needed, map and strip if enabled.
* <code>update</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Only update metadata. If false, only returned values will be set as metadata.
* <code>strip</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Completly remove empty metadata. Operates on both empty values and empty metadata chunk.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@rotate. rotate
<pre>(?id:string,?replay_metadata:bool,?track_sensitive:'a,
 ?transitions:[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)],
 ?weights:[int],[source('b)])->source('b)
where 'a is either bool or ()->bool</pre>

Rotate between the sources.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Replay the last metadata of a child when switching to it in the middle of a track.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>anything that is either bool or ()->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Re-select only on end of tracks.
* <code>transitions</code> (<code>[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Transition functions, padded with <code>fun (x,y) -> y</code> functions.
* <code>weights</code> (<code>[int]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Weights of the children (padded with 1), defining for each child how many tracks are played from it per round, if that many are actually available.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('b)]</code>)

h5@rotate_merge. rotate.merge
<pre>(?id:string,?track_sensitive:bool,
 ?transitions:[(source('a),source('a))->source('a)],
 ?weights:[int],[source('a)])->source('a)</pre>

Same operator as rotate but merges tracks from each sources.
For instance, <code>rotate.merge([intro,main,outro])</code> creates a source that plays a sequence <code>[intro,main,outro]</code> as single track and loops back.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Re-select only on end of tracks.
* <code>transitions</code> (<code>[(source('a),source('a))->source('a)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Transition functions, padded with <code>fun (x,y) -> y</code> functions.
* <code>weights</code> (<code>[int]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Weights of the children (padded with 1), defining for each child how many tracks are played from it per round, if that many are actually available.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('a)]</code>): Sequence of sources to be merged

h5@say_metadata. say_metadata
<pre>(source(?A),?pattern:string)->source(?A)</pre>

Append speech-synthesized tracks reading the metadata.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(?A)</code>): The source to use
* <code>pattern</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"say:$(if $(artist),\"It was $(artist)$(if $(title),\\\", $(title)\\\").\")"</code>): Pattern to use

h5@sequence. sequence
<pre>(?id:string,?merge:bool,[source('a)])->source('a)</pre>

Play only one track of every successive source, except for the last one which is played as much as available. Sources are released after being used, allowing them to shutdown cleanly and free their resources.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>merge</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Merge tracks when advancing from one source to the next one. This will NOT merge consecutive tracks from the last source; see merge_tracks() if you need that too.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('a)]</code>)

h5@server_insert_metadata. server.insert_metadata
<pre>(?id:string,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Register a server/telnet command to update a source's metadata. Returns a new source, which will receive the updated metadata. The command has the following format: insert key1="val1",key2="val2",...

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@skip_blank. skip_blank
<pre>(?id:string,?threshold:float,?max_blank:float,
 ?min_noise:float,?track_sensitive:bool,
 source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</pre>

Skip track when detecting a blank.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>threshold</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-40.0</code>): Power in decibels under which the stream is considered silent.
* <code>max_blank</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>20.0</code>): Maximum silence length allowed, in seconds.
* <code>min_noise</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Minimum duration of noise required to end silence, in seconds.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Reset blank counter at each track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi='#c)</code>)

h5@smart_crossfade. smart_crossfade
<pre>(?start_next:float,?fade_in:float,?fade_out:float,
 ?default:((source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0),
            source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
           source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)),
 ?high:float,?medium:float,?margin:float,?width:float,
 ?conservative:bool,source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Crossfade between tracks, taking the respective volume levels into account in the choice of the transition.

* <code>start_next</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>): Crossing duration, if any.
* <code>fade_in</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>3.0</code>): Fade-in duration, if any.
* <code>fade_out</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>3.0</code>): Fade-out duration, if any.
* <code>default</code> (<code>(source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0),
 source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</code> -- defaults to <code><fun></code>): Transition used when no rule applies (default: sequence).
* <code>high</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-15.0</code>): Value, in dB, for loud sound level.
* <code>medium</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-32.0</code>): Value, in dB, for medium sound level.
* <code>margin</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>4.0</code>): Margin to detect sources that have too different sound level for crossing.
* <code>width</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>2.0</code>): Width of the volume analysis window.
* <code>conservative</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Always prepare for a premature end-of-track.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#a+1,video=0,midi=0)</code>): The input source.

h5@smooth_add. smooth_add
<pre>(?delay:float,?p:float,
 normal:source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0),
 special:source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0))->
source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</pre>

Mixes two streams, with faded transitions between the state when only the normal stream is available and when the special stream gets added on top of it.

* <code>delay</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.5</code>): Delay before starting the special source.
* <code>p</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.2</code>): Portion of amplitude of the normal source in the mix.
* <code>normal</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</code>): The normal source, which could be called the carrier too.
* <code>special</code> (<code>source(audio='#a,video='#b,midi=0)</code>): The special source.

h5@switch. switch
<pre>(?id:string,?replay_metadata:bool,?single:[bool],
 ?track_sensitive:'a,
 ?transitions:[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)],
 [((()->bool)*source('b))])->source('b)
where 'a is either bool or ()->bool</pre>

At the beginning of a track, select the first source whose predicate is true.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>replay_metadata</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Replay the last metadata of a child when switching to it in the middle of a track.
* <code>single</code> (<code>[bool]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Forbid the selection of a branch for two tracks in a row. The empty list stands for <code>[false,...,false]</code>.
* <code>track_sensitive</code> (<code>anything that is either bool or ()->bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Re-select only on end of tracks.
* <code>transitions</code> (<code>[(source('b),source('b))->source('b)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Transition functions, padded with <code>fun (x,y) -> y</code> functions.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[((()->bool)*source('b))]</code>): Sources with the predicate telling when they can be played.

* <code>y</code> (<code>int</code> -- defaults to <code>-5</code>): y offset (negative means from bottom).

h5@video_fade_final. video.fade.final

h5@video_fade_in. video.fade.in

h5@video_frei0r__3dflippo. video.frei0r._3dflippo
<pre>(?id:string,?center_position:'a,?center_position:'b,
 ?don't_blank_mask:bool,?fill_with_image_or_black:bool,
 ?invert_rotation_assignment:bool,?x_axis_rotation:'c,
 ?x_axis_rotation_rate:'d,?y_axis_rotation:'e,
 ?y_axis_rotation_rate:'f,?z_axis_rotation:'g,
 ?z_axis_rotation_rate:'h,
 source(audio='#i,video='#j+1,midi='#k))->
source(audio='#i,video='#j+1,midi='#k)
where
  'a, 'b, 'c, 'd, 'e, 'f, 'g, 'h is either float or ()->float</pre>

Frame rotation in 3d-space (by c.e. prelz AS FLUIDO <fluido(at)fluido.as>).

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>center_position</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Position of the center of rotation on the X axis.
* <code>center_position</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Position of the center of rotation on the Y axis.
* <code>don't_blank_mask</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Mask for frame transposition is not blanked, so a trace of old transpositions is maintained.
* <code>fill_with_image_or_black</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): If true, pixels that are not transposed are black, otherwise, they are copied with the original.
* <code>invert_rotation_assignment</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): If true, when mapping rotation, make inverted (wrong) assignment.
* <code>x_axis_rotation</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.5</code>): Rotation on the X axis.

h5@video_frei0r_light_graffiti. video.frei0r.light_graffiti
<pre>(?id:string,?backgroundweight:'a,?blackreference:'b,
 ?dim:'c,?longalpha:'d,?loweroverexposure:'e,
 ?nonlineardim:'f,?reset:'g,?saturation:'h,
 ?sensitivity:'i,?statsbrightness:'j,?statsdifference:'k,
 ?statsdiffsum:'l,?thresholdbrightness:'m,
 ?thresholddifference:'n,?thresholddiffsum:'o,
 ?transparentbackground:'p,
 source(audio='#q,video='#r+1,midi='#s))->
source(audio='#q,video='#r+1,midi='#s)
where
  'a, 'b, 'c, 'd, 'e, 'f, 'g, 'h, 'i, 'j, 'k, 'l, 'm, 'n, 'o, 'p is either float or ()->float</pre>

Creates light graffitis from a video by keeping the brightest spots (by Simon A. Eugster (Granjow)).

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Force the value of the source ID.
* <code>backgroundweight</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Describes how strong the (accumulated) background should shine through.
* <code>blackreference</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Uses black as background image instead of the first frame..
* <code>dim</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Dimming of the light mask.
* <code>longalpha</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Alpha value for moving average.
* <code>loweroverexposure</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Prevents some overexposure if the light source stays steady too long (varying speed).
* <code>nonlineardim</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Nonlinear dimming (may look more natural).
* <code>reset</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Reset filter masks.
* <code>saturation</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.25</code>): Saturation of lights.
* <code>sensitivity</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.2</code>): Sensitivity of the effect for light (higher sensitivity will lead to brighter lights).
* <code>statsbrightness</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Display the brightness and threshold, for adjusting the brightness threshold parameter.
* <code>statsdifference</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Display the background difference and threshold.
* <code>statsdiffsum</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Display the sum of the background difference and the threshold.
* <code>thresholdbrightness</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.588235294118</code>): Brightness threshold to distinguish between foreground and background.
* <code>thresholddifference</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Threshold: Difference to background to distinguish between fore- and background.
* <code>thresholddiffsum</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Threshold for sum of differences. Can in most cases be ignored (set to 0)..
* <code>transparentbackground</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Make the background transparent.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source(audio='#q,video='#r+1,midi='#s)</code>)

* <code>amplitude</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.800000011921</code>): Amplitude (contrast) of the pattern.
* <code>aspect_type</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Pixel aspect ratio presets.
* <code>channel</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Into which color channel to draw.
* <code>freq_1</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0299999993294</code>): Pattern 7 H frequency.
* <code>freq_2</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0299999993294</code>): Pattern 7 V frequency.
* <code>lin_p_swp</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Use linear period sweep.
* <code>manual_aspect</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.5</code>): Manual pixel aspect ratio.
* <code>type</code> (<code>anything that is either float or ()->float</code> -- defaults to <code>0.0</code>): Type of test pattern.

h3@Control. Control
h5@add_timeout. add_timeout
<pre>(?fast:bool,float,(()->float))->unit</pre>

Call a function in N seconds. If the result of the function is positive or null, the task will be scheduled again after this amount of time (in seconds).

* <code>fast</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Set to <code>false</code> if the execution of the code can take long in order to lower its priority below that of request resolutions and fast timeouts. This is only effective if you set a dedicated queue for fast tasks, see the "scheduler" settings for more details.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>float</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>()->float</code>)

h5@ignore. ignore

h3@Liquidsoap. Liquidsoap
h5@add_decoder. add_decoder
<pre>(name:string,description:string,?mimes:[string],
 test:((string)->int),string)->unit</pre>

Register an external decoder. The encoder should output in WAV format to his standard output (stdout) and read data from its standard input (stdin).

* <code>name</code> (<code>string</code>): Format/decoder's name.
* <code>description</code> (<code>string</code>): Description of the decoder.
* <code>mimes</code> (<code>[string]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): List of mime types supported by this decoder for decoding streams.
* <code>test</code> (<code>(string)->int</code>): Function used to determine if a file should be decoded by the decoder. Returned values are: 0: no decodable audio, -1: decodable audio but number of audio channels unknown, x: fixed number of decodable audio channels.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Process to start.

h5@add_metadata_resolver. add_metadata_resolver
<pre>(string,((string)->[(string*string)]))->unit</pre>

Register an external file metadata decoder.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Format/resolver's name.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(string)->[(string*string)]</code>): Process to start. The function takes the format and filename as argument and returns a list of (name,value) fields.

h5@add_oblivious_decoder. add_oblivious_decoder
<pre>(name:string,description:string,test:((string)->int),
 ?buffer:float,((string)->string))->unit</pre>

Register an external file decoder. The encoder should output in WAV format to his standard output (stdout) and read data from the file it receives. The estimated remaining duration for this decoder will be unknown until the @buffer@ last seconds of the file. If possible, it is recommended to decode from stdin and use @add_decoder@.

* <code>name</code> (<code>string</code>): Format/decoder's name.
* <code>description</code> (<code>string</code>): Description of the decoder.
* <code>test</code> (<code>(string)->int</code>): Function used to determine if a file should be decoded by the decoder. Returned values are: 0: no decodable audio, -1: decodable audio but number of audio channels unknown, x: fixed number of decodable audio channels.
* <code>buffer</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>5.0</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(string)->string</code>): Process to start. The function takes the filename as argument and returns the process to start.

h5@add_playlist_parser. add_playlist_parser
<pre>(format:string,strict:bool,
 ((?pwd:string,string)->[([(string*string)]*string)]))->
unit</pre>

Register a new playlist parser.

* <code>format</code> (<code>string</code>): Playlist format. If possible, a mime-type.
* <code>strict</code> (<code>bool</code>): True if playlist format can be detected unambiguously.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(?pwd:string,string)->[([(string*string)]*string)]</code>): Playlist parser

h5@add_protocol. add_protocol
<pre>(?temporary:bool,?static:bool,?syntax:string,?doc:string,
 string,
 ((rlog:((string)->unit),maxtime:float,string)->[string]))->
unit</pre>

Register a new protocol.

* <code>temporary</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): if true, file is removed when it is finished.
* <code>static</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): if true, then requests can be resolved once and for all. Typically, static protocols can be used to create infallible sources.
* <code>syntax</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Undocumented"</code>): URI syntax.
* <code>doc</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"Undocumented"</code>): Protocol documentation.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Protocol name. Resolver will be called on uris of the form: @<protocol name>:...@.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(rlog:((string)->unit),maxtime:float,string)->[string]</code>): Protocol resolver. Receives a function to log protocol resolution, the @<arg>@ in @<protocol name>:<arg>@ and the max delay that resolution should take.

h5@clock. clock
<pre>(?sync:bool,?id:string,source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Assign a new clock to the given source (and to other time-dependent sources) and return the source. It is a conveniency wrapper around clock.assign_new(), allowing more concise scripts in some cases.

* <code>sync</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Do not synchronize the clock on regular wallclock time, but try to run as fast as possible (CPU burning mode).
* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@clock_assign_new. clock.assign_new
<pre>(?id:string,?sync:bool,[source('a)])->unit</pre>

Create a new clock and assign it to a list of sources.

* <code>id</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>): Identifier for the new clock. The default empty string means that the identifier of the first source will be used.
* <code>sync</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Do not synchronize the clock on regular wallclock time, but try to run as fast as possible (CPU burning mode).
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>[source('a)]</code>): List of sources to which the new clock will be assigned

h5@enable_external_faad_decoder. enable_external_faad_decoder
<pre>()->unit</pre>

Enable or disable external FAAD (AAC/AAC+/M4A) decoders.  Requires faad binary in the path for audio decoding and metaflac binary for metadata. Does not work on Win32.
Please note that built-in support for faad is available in liquidsoap if compiled and should be preferred over the external decoder.


h5@enable_external_flac_decoder. enable_external_flac_decoder
<pre>()->unit</pre>

Please note that built-in support for FLAC is available in liquidsoap if compiled and should be preferred over the external decoder.

* <code>extract_replaygain</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"/usr/local/lib/liquidsoap/scm/extract-replaygain"</code>): The extraction program

h5@harbor_http_register. harbor.http.register
<pre>(port:int,method:string,string,
 ((protocol:string,data:string,headers:[(string*string)],
   string)->string))->unit</pre>

Register a HTTP handler on the harbor. The given function receives as argument the full requested uri (e.g. "foo?var=bar"), http protocol version, possible input data and the list of HTTP headers and returns the answer sent to the client, including HTTP headers. Registered uri can be regular expressions (e.g. ".+\.php") and can override default metadata handlers.

* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code>): Port to server.
* <code>method</code> (<code>string</code>): Accepted method
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URI to serve.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>(protocol:string,data:string,headers:[(string*string)],
 string)->string</code>): Function to execute. method argument is "PUT" or "GET", protocol argument is "HTTP/1.1" or "HTTP/1.0" etc., data argument contains data passed in case of a PUT request, and "" otherwise. headers argument contains the HTTP headers. Unlabeled argument contains the requested URI.

h5@harbor_http_remove. harbor.http.remove
<pre>(method:string,port:int,string)->unit</pre>

Remove a registered HTTP handler on the harbor.

* <code>method</code> (<code>string</code>): Method served.
* <code>port</code> (<code>int</code>): Port to server.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): URI served.

h5@register_flow. register_flow
<pre>(?server:string,?user:string,?password:string,
 ?email:string,radio:string,website:string,
 description:string,genre:string,
 streams:[(string*string)],source('a))->source('a)</pre>

Register a radio on Liquidsoap Flows.

* <code>server</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>user</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>"default"</code>)

* <code>email</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>radio</code> (<code>string</code>): Name of the radio.
* <code>website</code> (<code>string</code>): URL of the website of the radio.
* <code>description</code> (<code>string</code>): Description of the radio.
* <code>genre</code> (<code>string</code>): Genre of the radio (rock or rap or etc.).
* <code>streams</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code>): List of streams for the radio described by a pair of strings consisting of the format of the stream and the url of the stream. The format should be of the form "ogg/128k" consisting of the codec and the bitrate, separated by "/".
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>source('a)</code>)

h5@request_create. request.create

h5@request_create_raw. request.create.raw
<pre>(?indicators:[string],?persistent:bool,string)->
request(audio=0,video=0,midi=0)</pre>

Create a raw request, i.e. for files that should not be decoded for streaming. Creation may fail if there is no available RID, which cannot be detected currently: in that case one will obtain a request that will fail to be resolved.

* <code>indicators</code> (<code>[string]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>)
* <code>persistent</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>)

h5@request_destroy. request.destroy
<pre>(?force:bool,request('a))->unit</pre>

Destroying a request causes any temporary associated file to be deleted, and releases its RID. Persistent requests resist to destroying, unless forced.

* <code>force</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>false</code>): Destroy the request even if it is persistent.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>request('a)</code>)

h5@request_ready. request.ready

h5@request_resolve. request.resolve
<pre>(?timeout:float,request('a))->bool</pre>

* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>30.0</code>): Limit in seconds to the duration of the resolving.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>request('a)</code>)

h5@exec_at. exec_at
<pre>(?freq:float,pred:(()->bool),(()->unit))->unit</pre>

Execute a given action when a predicate is true. This will be run in background.

* <code>freq</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>1.0</code>): Frequency for checking the predicate, in seconds.
* <code>pred</code> (<code>()->bool</code>): Predicate indicating when to execute the function, typically a time interval such as <code>{10h-10h30}</code>.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>()->unit</code>): Function to execute when the predicate is true.

h5@exit. exit
<pre>(int)->unit</pre>

Immediately stop the application. This should only be used in extreme cases or to specify an exit value. The recommended way of stopping Liquidsoap is to use shutdown.

* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>int</code>): Exit value.

<pre>(?timeout:float,?env:[(string*string)],?inherit_env:bool,
 string)->[string]</pre>

* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Cancel process after @timeout@ has elapsed. Ignored if negative.
* <code>env</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Process environment
* <code>inherit_env</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Inherit calling process's environment when @env@ parameter is empty.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Command to run

h5@getopt. getopt
<pre>(?default:string,string)->string</pre>

Parse command line options:
<code>getopt("-o")</code> returns "1" if "-o" was passed without any parameter, "0" otherwise.
<code>getopt(default="X","-o")</code> returns "Y" if "-o Y" was passed, "X" otherwise.
The result is removed from the list of arguments, affecting subsequent
calls to <code>argv()</code> and <code>getopt()</code>.

* <code>default</code> (<code>string</code> -- defaults to <code>""</code>)
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>)

h5@run_process. run_process
<pre>(?env:[(string*string)],?inherit_env:bool,?timeout:float,
 string)->((string*string)*(string*string))</pre>

Run a process in a shell environment. Returns: @((stdout,stderr),status)@ where status is one of: @("exit","<code>")@, @("killed","<signal number>")@, @("stopped","<signal number>")@, @("exception","<exception description>", @("timeout","<run time>")@.

* <code>env</code> (<code>[(string*string)]</code> -- defaults to <code>[]</code>): Process environment
* <code>inherit_env</code> (<code>bool</code> -- defaults to <code>true</code>): Inherit calling process's environment when @env@ parameter is empty.
* <code>timeout</code> (<code>float</code> -- defaults to <code>-1.0</code>): Cancel process after @timeout@ has elapsed. Ignored if negative.
* <code>(unlabeled)</code> (<code>string</code>): Command to run
